USFI_Air_Support_Initialize = {
	set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Begun
	clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag
	set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 0 }
	set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Health = 100 }
	set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score_to_Reach = 1000 }
	set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_AI_Refresh_Units_Counter = 0 }

USFI_Air_Support_Clear_Guns = {
	clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected
	clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected
	clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Selected
}

USFI_Air_Support_Set_Guns_Frame = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Button_Frame = 2 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Button_Frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Button_Frame = 1 }
		
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - 25mm Selected"
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Button_Frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Button_Frame = 2 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Button_Frame = 1 }
		
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - 40mm Selected"
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Selected }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Button_Frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Button_Frame = 1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Button_Frame = 2 }
		
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - 105mm Selected"
	}
	
	USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes
}

USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count < 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Disabled }
		}
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Disabled
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Reload_Counter = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count < 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Disabled }
		}
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Disabled
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Reload_Counter = 0 }
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Ammo_Count < 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Disabled }
		}
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Disabled
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Reload_Counter = 0 }
	}
}

USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = {
	add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_dirty = 1 }
}

USFI_Air_Support_Increase_Level = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_9 }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score_to_Reach = 1000000 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Tick_TRIGGER = 12 }
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Already at L9"
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_8 }
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_8
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score_to_Reach = 16000 }
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_9
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_AI_Refresh_Units_Counter = 0 }
		set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_Text_visible_flag
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Tick_TRIGGER = 16 }
		USFI_Air_Support_Setup_Level_9 = yes
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Game is at L9"
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_7 }

USFI_Air_Support_AI_Tick = {
	
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Reloading Pulse"
	
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Disabled }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Reload_Counter = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Reload_Counter = 3 } }
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Disabled
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 75 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected }
				clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Disabled }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Reload_Counter = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Reload_Counter = 6 } }
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Disabled
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 12 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected }
				clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Disabled }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Reload_Counter = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Reload_Counter = 9 } }
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Disabled
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Ammo_Count = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Selected }
				clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire
			}
		}
	}

	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Movement Pulse"
	
	### Infantry1 ###
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_Visible }
		
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Move Infantry1"
		
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos_Change }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos_Change }
		
		if = { # Out of Bounds Check
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos > 3840 }
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos < 0 }
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos > 2160 }
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos < 0 }
				}
			}
			USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_Minus = yes
		}
	}
	### Infantry1 ###
	### Infantry2 ###
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry2_Visible }
		
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Move Infantry2"
		
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry2_XPos = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry2_XPos_Change }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry2_YPos = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry2_YPos_Change }

		if = { # Out of Bounds Check
			limit = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Tank11_XPos > 3840 }
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Tank11_XPos < 0 }
					check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Tank11_YPos > 2160 }

		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Tick = USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Tick_TRIGGER } }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Health = 20 }
			sound_effect = "usfi_boom"
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Loss = yes
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Tick = 0 }
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag 
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag }
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag
			sound_effect = "usfi_beep"
		}
	}
	### SAM Turret ###
	
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Reload Enemies Pulse"

	}
	
	USFI_Air_Support_Check_Level_Up = yes
	USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes

USFI_Air_Support_Check_Level_Up = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score > USFI_Air_Support_Score_to_Reach }
		}
		USFI_Air_Support_Increase_Level = yes
	}
}

USFI_Air_Support_Check_Loss = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Health < 1 }
		}
		play_song = "general_peace_1"
		
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_visible
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Title_visible
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Begun
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag
		
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_9
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_8
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_7
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_6
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_5
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_4
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_3
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_2
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_1
	}
}

USFI_Air_Support_End_Game = {
	AAO_CIA_Air_Support_Give_Buff = yes
	
	set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Health = 0 }
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Health < 1 }
		}
		play_song = "general_peace_1"
		
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_visible
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Title_visible
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Begun
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_GUI_Level_Up_Notif_SAM_Text_visible_flag
		
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_9
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_8
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_7
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_6
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_5
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_4
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_3
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_2
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_1
	}
}

AAO_CIA_Air_Support_Give_Buff = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_9 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.9 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.9 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_8 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.8 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.8 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_7 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.7 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.7 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 30 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_6 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.6 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.6 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_5 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.5 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.5 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_4 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.4 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.4 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 20 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_3 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.3 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.3 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_2 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.2 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.2 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 10 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Mission_Level_1 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.1 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.1 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 10 }
	}
	else = {
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_breakthrough_factor = 0.01 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_initiative_factor = 0.01 }
		set_variable = { AAO_Gunship_Support_days = 1 }
	}
	
	add_dynamic_modifier = {
		modifier = AAO_Gunship_Support
		days = var:AAO_Gunship_Support_days
	}
}

### Click Actions ###

USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_Plus = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire } }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 100 }
		# play anim at coords
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_Visible
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 5 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_2" } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 3 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_2" } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Selected }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Ammo_Count = 1 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_105mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_105mm_2" } }
		}
		USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
		
		USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes
	}
}

	#subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 50 }
	clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_Visible
	
	USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes
}

		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire } }
		add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 100 }
		# play anim at coords
		clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry19_Visible
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 5 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_2" } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 3 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_2" } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Selected }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Ammo_Count = 1 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_105mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_105mm_2" } }
		}
		USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
		
		USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes
	}
}

	#subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 50 }
	clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Infantry19_Visible
	
	USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes
}

USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Plus = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 5 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Hit_1 }
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 3 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Hit_1
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Frame = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Hit_1
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 500 }
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Frame = 1 }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 3 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			# play anim at coords
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Visible
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Hit_1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_105MM_Selected
			}
			add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 500 }
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Frame = 1 }
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_105MM_Ammo_Count = 1 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_105mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_105mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			# play anim at coords
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Visible
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Tank1_Hit_1
		}
		
		USFI_Air_Support_Redraw_GUI = yes
	}
}

			set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Frame = 2 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_2 }
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 5 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_2
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Frame = 3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_2
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 5 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 1000 }
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Frame = 1 }
			# play anim at coords
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_2
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Visible
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1 }
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 3 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			set_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Frame = 3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_40MM_Selected
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_40MM_Ammo_Count = 3 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_40mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes
			add_to_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Score = 1000 }
			set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Frame = 1 }
			# play anim at coords
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Hit_1
			clr_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Heli6_Visible
		}
		else_if = {

	}

USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Plus = {
	if = {
		limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_Cant_Fire } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_25MM_Selected
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Hit_1 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = USFI_Air_Support_SAM_Hit_2 }
				}
			}
			subtract_from_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_GUI_25MM_Ammo_Count = 5 }
			random_list = { 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_1" } 50 = { sound_effect = "usfi_25mm_2" } }
			USFI_Air_Support_Check_Reload = yes

### Unit Randomizer ###

USFI_Air_Support_Get_Random_Movement_Infantry1 = {
	log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: USFI Air Support - Generating new Infantry1"
	set_temp_variable = { Random_X = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { Random_Y = 0 }
	set_variable = { Random_Speed = 0 }
	set_variable = { Random_Direction = 0 }
	randomize_temp_variable = {
		var = Random_X
		distribution = uniform
		min = 50
		max = 3800
	}
	randomize_temp_variable = {
		var = Random_Y
		distribution = uniform
		min = 50
		max = 2100
	}
	randomize_temp_variable = {
		var = Random_Speed
		distribution = uniform
		min = 5
		max = 15
	}
	randomize_temp_variable = { # 0 = L-->R, 1 = L<--R, 2 = T-->B, 3 = T<--B
		var = Random_Direction
		distribution = uniform
		min = 0
		max = 3
	}
	round_temp_variable = Random_X
	round_temp_variable = Random_Y
	round_temp_variable = Random_Speed
	round_temp_variable = Random_Direction
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { Random_Direction = 0 } }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos = 1 } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos = Random_Y } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos_Change = Random_Speed } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos_Change = 0 } 
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { Random_Direction = 1 } }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos = 3839 } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos = Random_Y }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Random_Speed = -1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos_Change = Random_Speed } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos_Change = 0 } 
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { Random_Direction = 2 } }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos = Random_X } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos = 1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos_Change = 0 } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos_Change = Random_Speed } 
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { Random_Direction = 3 } }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos = Random_X } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos = 2159 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { Random_Speed = -1 }
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_XPos_Change = 0 } 
		set_variable = { USFI_Air_Support_Infantry1_YPos_Change = Random_Speed } 
	}
	else = {
		USFI_Air_Support_Get_Random_Movement_Infantry1 = yes
	}
}
